## Instruction

I am a male university student, and my detailed body information is in `body.md`. I plan to create a fitness plan for the next 3 months, and I am currently at the initial stage of fat loss. Please help me analyze the dietary list of my rest day (located in `cuisine.md`, with all dishes eaten in one portion, use info from howtocook) to determine whether it meets the nutritional requirements of carbohydrates and protein. The nutritional composition of various raw ingredients is provided in `Nutrition.xlsx`, and the fitness dietary guidelines are in `health_guide.md`. Please follow exactly the instructions in format.md to give your nutritional analysis of the foods and record it in a newly created `analysis.md` file.

```json output_result
# Experienced Dietary Ratios for Muscle Gain and Fat Loss

Unit: g = daily intake per kg of body weight (g/kg)

| Type          | Cycle         | Carbs (g/kg)  | Protein (g/kg) |
| :------------ | :------------ | :------------ | :------------- |
| **Muscle Gain** | Male          | 3.5-4.5       | 1.5-2          |
|               | Female        | 3-3.5         | 1.5            |
| **Fat Loss** | Male (Initial)| 2.5-3         | 1.5            |
|               | Male (Late)   | 2-2.5         | 1.2-1.5        |
|               | Female (Initial)| 2.5-3         | 1.5            |
|               | Female (Late) | 2-2.5         | 1.2-1.5        |

---

**Adjustment Methods (Carbs as Calorie Variable):**

1.  **For muscle gain, try for 2 weeks**. Adjust if weight increases by about 1%.
    Reduce carbs if gaining too fast, increase carbs if gaining too slow. Adjust carbs by about 0.5g.

2.  **For fat loss, try for 2 weeks**. Adjust if weight decreases by about 2%.
    Reduce carbs if losing too slow, increase carbs if losing too fast. Adjust carbs by about 0.5g.
    There's more room for rapid carb reduction from the initial to late stages of fat loss, but don't rush.

3.  **No need to recalculate ratios after small weight changes**, as it's only a few grams difference.
    No need to recalculate during the muscle gain phase. During the fat loss phase, you can recalculate once after losing 5-10 kg.

---

**Notes (For Large-Bodied Obese Individuals):**

* **For large-bodied obese individuals with BMI > 28**, reduce initial carb intake during the fat loss phase (Male 2.4-2.7g, Female 2.1-2.4g), reduce protein (Male 1.2g), and reduce fat (Male 0.6g).
* **For large-bodied obese individuals with BMI > 32**, reduce initial carb intake during the fat loss phase (Male 2.0-2.4g, Female 1.7-2.0g), reduce protein (Male 1.0g), and reduce fat (Male 0.5g).
* **The above table refers to training days**. On rest days, reduce carb intake (by 0.5g compared to training days).

**Note: Protein intake can fluctuate by +/- 10g from the allocated amount and still be within expectations. Carbohydrate intake must be strictly controlled within the given range.**
```

```json output_result
# Analysis Output Format Guide

Please follow this EXACT format for your nutritional analysis.

## Required Format:


# Today's Meal Nutritional Analysis

- **Carbohydrates**: [Assessment]. Expected: [range] | Actual: [calculated value]

- **Protein**: [Assessment]. Expected: [target] | Actual: [calculated value]


## Assessment Options:
- **Below expectations** -  the actual intake is under 95% of the lower bound of the target range
- **Excessive intake** - the actual intake is over 105% of the upper bound of the target range
- **Meets expectations** - otherwise

## Format Examples:

**Example 1:**

# Today's Meal Nutritional Analysis

- **Carbohydrates**: Below expectations. Expected: 162.5g-195g | Actual: 135.5g

- **Protein**: Excessive intake. Expected: 97.5g | Actual: 146.9g


**Example 2:**

# Today's Meal Nutritional Analysis

- **Carbohydrates**: Meets expectations. Expected: 162.5g-195g | Actual: 175g

- **Protein**: Meets expectations. Expected: 97.5g | Actual: 98g


## Important Notes:
- Use **exactly** this heading: "# Today's Meal Nutritional Analysis"
- Include both "Expected:" and "Actual:" values
- The "|" separator between Expected and Actual is required
- Use the average nutrient value when the ingredient amount is provided as a range
```

</Expandable>

```python
import json

# Body information
height_cm = 152
weight_kg = 65

# Calculate BMI
bmi = weight_kg / ((height_cm / 100) ** 2)
print(f"BMI: {bmi:.2f}")

# Dietary requirements for male, initial fat loss stage, rest day
# According to health_guide.md:
# - Carbs: 2.5-3 g/kg for training days, reduce by 0.5g for rest days = 2.0-2.5 g/kg
# - Protein: 1.5 g/kg
# Note: For BMI > 28, adjustments apply
if bmi > 28:
    carbs_min = 2.4 - 0.5  # 1.9 g/kg for rest day
    carbs_max = 2.7 - 0.5  # 2.2 g/kg for rest day
    protein_target = 1.2
else:
    carbs_min = 2.5 - 0.5  # 2.0 g/kg for rest day
    carbs_max = 3.0 - 0.5  # 2.5 g/kg for rest day
    protein_target = 1.5

expected_carbs_min = carbs_min * weight_kg
expected_carbs_max = carbs_max * weight_kg
expected_protein = protein_target * weight_kg

print(f"\nExpected daily intake:")
print(f"Carbohydrates: {expected_carbs_min:.1f}g - {expected_carbs_max:.1f}g")
print(f"Protein: {expected_protein:.1f}g")

# Recipe ingredients (1 portion each)
# 西红柿炒鸡蛋 (Breakfast)
# Based on recipe: 1 tomato (180g), 1.5 eggs (75g), 4ml oil per egg (6ml total), 1.5-2g salt, 0-2g sugar
breakfast_ingredients = {
    "西红柿": 180,  # 1个
    "鸡蛋": 75,     # 1.5个 (50g each)
    "植物油": 6,    # 6ml = 5.52g (1ml≈0.92g)
    "盐": 1.75,     # average of 1.5-2g
    "白砂糖": 1     # average of 0-2g
}

# 荔枝肉 (Lunch) - 1 portion
# Based on recipe: 瘦肉150g, 凤梨100g, 鸡蛋1个(50g), 食用油500ml(but mostly for frying, absorbed ~30ml=27.6g), 
# 白砂糖5g, 淀粉100g(but coating, absorbed ~20g), 生抽5ml, 鸡精5g, 姜末5g, 芝麻2g, 番茄酱20g, 香醋2ml
lunch_ingredients = {
    "瘦肉(猪肉)": 150,
    "凤梨(菠萝)": 100,
    "鸡蛋": 50,
    "植物油": 27.6,  # estimated absorbed oil (30ml * 0.92)
    "白砂糖": 5,
    "淀粉": 20,      # estimated absorbed starch
    "蒸鱼豉油": 5,   # using this as soy sauce proxy (5ml * 1.1 = 5.5g)
    "鸡精": 5,
    "姜": 5,
    "芝麻": 2,
    "西红柿": 20,    # tomato sauce proxy
    "香醋": 2.1,     # 2ml * 1.05
    "蟹味菇": 30,
}

# 葱油桂鱼 (Dinner) - 1 portion
# Based on recipe: 桂鱼500g, 小葱30cm(~30g), 小米辣2个(~10g), 姜50g, 料酒25g, 植物油15g, 盐8g, 蒸鱼豉油10g
dinner_ingredients = {
    "桂鱼": 500,
    "蒜": 30,        # using garlic as proxy for scallion
    "青椒": 10,      # using green pepper as proxy for chili
    "姜": 50,
    "植物油": 15,
    "盐": 8,
    "蒸鱼豉油": 11   # 10g
}

# Nutrition data mapping (per 100g)
nutrition_db = {
    "西红柿": {"carbs": 3.9, "protein": 0.9},
    "鸡蛋": {"carbs": 1.1, "protein": 13.3},
    "植物油": {"carbs": 0, "protein": 0},
    "盐": {"carbs": 0, "protein": 0},
    "白砂糖": {"carbs": 99.9, "protein": 0},
    "瘦肉(猪肉)": {"carbs": 0, "protein": 20.3},
    "凤梨(菠萝)": {"carbs": 13.1, "protein": 0.5},
    "淀粉": {"carbs": 85, "protein": 0.2},
    "蒸鱼豉油": {"carbs": 10.2, "protein": 8.3},
    "鸡精": {"carbs": 24.5, "protein": 9.3},
    "姜": {"carbs": 7.8, "protein": 1.8},
    "芝麻": {"carbs": 23.4, "protein": 19.1},
    "香醋": {"carbs": 2.1, "protein": 2.1},
    "蟹味菇": {"carbs": 5.1, "protein": 2.1},
    "桂鱼": {"carbs": 0, "protein": 18.6},
    "蒜": {"carbs": 26.5, "protein": 4.5},
    "青椒": {"carbs": 5.4, "protein": 1.0},
}

def calculate_nutrition(ingredients, nutrition_db):
    total_carbs = 0
    total_protein = 0
    
    for ingredient, amount_g in ingredients.items():
        if ingredient in nutrition_db:
            nutrient = nutrition_db[ingredient]
            total_carbs += (nutrient["carbs"] * amount_g) / 100
            total_protein += (nutrient["protein"] * amount_g) / 100
    
    return total_carbs, total_protein

# Calculate for each meal
breakfast_carbs, breakfast_protein = calculate_nutrition(breakfast_ingredients, nutrition_db)
lunch_carbs, lunch_protein = calculate_nutrition(lunch_ingredients, nutrition_db)
dinner_carbs, dinner_protein = calculate_nutrition(dinner_ingredients, nutrition_db)

print(f"\n=== Meal Breakdown ===")
print(f"Breakfast (西红柿炒鸡蛋):")
print(f"  Carbs: {breakfast_carbs:.1f}g, Protein: {breakfast_protein:.1f}g")
print(f"Lunch (荔枝肉):")
print(f"  Carbs: {lunch_carbs:.1f}g, Protein: {lunch_protein:.1f}g")
print(f"Dinner (葱油桂鱼):")
print(f"  Carbs: {dinner_carbs:.1f}g, Protein: {dinner_protein:.1f}g")

# Total daily intake
total_carbs = breakfast_carbs + lunch_carbs + dinner_carbs
total_protein = breakfast_protein + lunch_protein + dinner_protein

print(f"\n=== Total Daily Intake ===")
print(f"Total Carbohydrates: {total_carbs:.1f}g")
print(f"Total Protein: {total_protein:.1f}g")

# Assessment
def assess_nutrient(actual, min_val, max_val):
    lower_threshold = min_val * 0.95
    upper_threshold = max_val * 1.05
    
    if actual < lower_threshold:
        return "Below expectations"
    elif actual > upper_threshold:
        return "Excessive intake"
    else:
        return "Meets expectations"

carbs_assessment = assess_nutrient(total_carbs, expected_carbs_min, expected_carbs_max)
protein_assessment = assess_nutrient(total_protein, expected_protein, expected_protein)

print(f"\n=== Assessment ===")
print(f"Carbohydrates: {carbs_assessment}")
print(f"Protein: {protein_assessment}")

# Generate analysis.md content
analysis_content = f"""# Today's Meal Nutritional Analysis

- **Carbohydrates**: {carbs_assessment}. Expected: {expected_carbs_min:.1f}g-{expected_carbs_max:.1f}g | Actual: {total_carbs:.1f}g

- **Protein**: {protein_assessment}. Expected: {expected_protein:.1f}g | Actual: {total_protein:.1f}g"""

print(f"\n=== Analysis Content ===")
print(analysis_content)

# Save to variable for file writing
with open('/tmp/analysis_content.txt', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    f.write(analysis_content)

print("\nAnalysis content saved to /tmp/analysis_content.txt")
 code
```

- Carbs: 62.9g | Protein: 147.7g

### Assessment:
- **Carbohydrates**: **Below expectations** - You're consuming only 62.9g, which is significantly below the expected range of 123.5g-143.0g. You need to add more carbohydrate sources like rice, noodles, or whole grains to meet your energy needs.

- **Protein**: **Excessive intake** - You're consuming 147.7g, which is nearly double the expected 78.0g. While protein is important, excessive intake may not be optimal for fat loss.

### Recommendations:
1. **Increase carbohydrates**: Add rice, sweet potatoes, or whole grain staples to your meals
2. **Reduce protein portions**: Consider smaller portions of meat/fish or fewer protein-rich dishes
3. **Balance your meals**: Aim for a more balanced macronutrient distribution across all three meals

```json output_result
# Experienced Dietary Ratios for Muscle Gain and Fat Loss

Unit: g = daily intake per kg of body weight (g/kg)

| Type          | Cycle         | Carbs (g/kg)  | Protein (g/kg) |
| :------------ | :------------ | :------------ | :------------- |
| **Muscle Gain** | Male          | 3.5-4.5       | 1.5-2          |
|               | Female        | 3-3.5         | 1.5            |
| **Fat Loss** | Male (Initial)| 2.5-3         | 1.5            |
|               | Male (Late)   | 2-2.5         | 1.2-1.5        |
|               | Female (Initial)| 2.5-3         | 1.5            |
|               | Female (Late) | 2-2.5         | 1.2-1.5        |

---

**Adjustment Methods (Carbs as Calorie Variable):**

1.  **For muscle gain, try for 2 weeks**. Adjust if weight increases by about 1%.
    Reduce carbs if gaining too fast, increase carbs if gaining too slow. Adjust carbs by about 0.5g.

2.  **For fat loss, try for 2 weeks**. Adjust if weight decreases by about 2%.
    Reduce carbs if losing too slow, increase carbs if losing too fast. Adjust carbs by about 0.5g.
    There's more room for rapid carb reduction from the initial to late stages of fat loss, but don't rush.

3.  **No need to recalculate ratios after small weight changes**, as it's only a few grams difference.
    No need to recalculate during the muscle gain phase. During the fat loss phase, you can recalculate once after losing 5-10 kg.

---

**Notes (For Large-Bodied Obese Individuals):**

* **For large-bodied obese individuals with BMI > 28**, reduce initial carb intake during the fat loss phase (Male 2.4-2.7g, Female 2.1-2.4g), reduce protein (Male 1.2g), and reduce fat (Male 0.6g).
* **For large-bodied obese individuals with BMI > 32**, reduce initial carb intake during the fat loss phase (Male 2.0-2.4g, Female 1.7-2.0g), reduce protein (Male 1.0g), and reduce fat (Male 0.5g).
* **The above table refers to training days**. On rest days, reduce carb intake (by 0.5g compared to training days).

**Note: Protein intake can fluctuate by +/- 10g from the allocated amount and still be within expectations. Carbohydrate intake must be strictly controlled within the given range.**
```

</Expandable>
</div>

```json output_result
# Analysis Output Format Guide

Please follow this EXACT format for your nutritional analysis.

## Required Format:


# Today's Meal Nutritional Analysis

- **Carbohydrates**: [Assessment]. Expected: [range] | Actual: [calculated value]

- **Protein**: [Assessment]. Expected: [target] | Actual: [calculated value]


## Assessment Options:
- **Below expectations** -  the actual intake is under 95% of the lower bound of the target range
- **Excessive intake** - the actual intake is over 105% of the upper bound of the target range
- **Meets expectations** - otherwise

## Format Examples:

**Example 1:**

# Today's Meal Nutritional Analysis

- **Carbohydrates**: Below expectations. Expected: 162.5g-195g | Actual: 135.5g

- **Protein**: Excessive intake. Expected: 97.5g | Actual: 146.9g


**Example 2:**

# Today's Meal Nutritional Analysis

- **Carbohydrates**: Meets expectations. Expected: 162.5g-195g | Actual: 175g

- **Protein**: Meets expectations. Expected: 97.5g | Actual: 98g


## Important Notes:
- Use **exactly** this heading: "# Today's Meal Nutritional Analysis"
- Include both "Expected:" and "Actual:" values
- The "|" separator between Expected and Actual is required
- Use the average nutrient value when the ingredient amount is provided as a range
```

```python
# Calculate BMI and nutritional requirements
height = 152  # cm
weight = 65   # kg

# Calculate BMI
height_m = height / 100
bmi = weight / (height_m ** 2)
print(f"Height: {height}cm, Weight: {weight}kg")
print(f"BMI: {bmi:.1f}")

# According to health_guide.md:
# Fat Loss (Male Initial): Carbs 2.5-3 g/kg, Protein 1.5 g/kg
# On rest days: reduce carb intake by 0.5g compared to training days

# Training day carbs: 2.5-3 g/kg
# Rest day carbs: (2.5-0.5) to (3-0.5) = 2.0-2.5 g/kg
rest_day_carbs_min = 2.0 * weight
rest_day_carbs_max = 2.5 * weight
protein_target = 1.5 * weight

print(f"\nRest Day Nutritional Targets:")
print(f"Carbohydrates: {rest_day_carbs_min:.1f}g - {rest_day_carbs_max:.1f}g")
print(f"Protein: {protein_target:.1f}g") code
```

<Expandable title="Details">
```python
# Create a dictionary of nutritional data from the Excel file
# Based on the Excel data I read earlier

nutrition_data = {
    "西红柿": {"carbs": 3.9, "protein": 0.9},  # 西红柿 (tomato)
    "鸡蛋": {"carbs": 1.1, "protein": 13.3},  # 鸡蛋 (egg)
    "食用油": {"carbs": 0, "protein": 0},  # 食用油 (cooking oil)
    "盐": {"carbs": 0, "protein": 0},  # 盐 (salt)
    "糖": {"carbs": 99.9, "protein": 0},  # 糖 (sugar)
    "葱花": {"carbs": 3.7, "protein": 2.0},  # 香葱 (scallion)
    "瘦肉": {"carbs": 0, "protein": 20.3},  # 瘦肉 (lean pork)
    "凤梨": {"carbs": 13.1, "protein": 0.5},  # 凤梨 (pineapple)
    "淀粉": {"carbs": 85, "protein": 0.2},  # 淀粉 (starch)
    "生抽": {"carbs": 10.2, "protein": 8.3},  # 蒸鱼豉油/生抽 (soy sauce)
    "鸡精": {"carbs": 24.5, "protein": 9.3},  # 鸡精 (chicken essence)
    "姜": {"carbs": 7.8, "protein": 1.8},  # 姜 (ginger)
    "芝麻": {"carbs": 23.4, "protein": 19.1},  # 芝麻 (sesame)
    "番茄酱": {"carbs": 24.5, "protein": 9.3},  # 番茄酱 (tomato sauce)
    "香醋": {"carbs": 2.1, "protein": 2.1},  # 香醋 (vinegar)
    "鲜香菇": {"carbs": 5.1, "protein": 2.1},  # 鲜香菇 (fresh shiitake)
    "蟹味菇": {"carbs": 5.1, "protein": 2.1},  # 蟹味菇 (crab mushroom)
    "桂鱼": {"carbs": 0, "protein": 18.6},  # 桂鱼 (mandarin fish)
    "小葱": {"carbs": 3.7, "protein": 2.0},  # 小葱 (scallion)
    "小米辣": {"carbs": 5.4, "protein": 1.0},  # 青椒 (green pepper)
    "料酒": {"carbs": 2.1, "protein": 2.1},  # 料酒 (cooking wine)
    "植物油": {"carbs": 0, "protein": 0},  # 植物油 (vegetable oil)
    "蒸鱼豉油": {"carbs": 10.2, "protein": 8.3},  # 蒸鱼豉油 (steamed fish soy sauce)
}

# Calculate nutritional content for each dish
# Using standard portion sizes from recipes

def calculate_dish_nutrition(ingredients_dict):
    total_carbs = 0
    total_protein = 0
    
    for ingredient, amount in ingredients_dict.items():
        if ingredient in nutrition_data:
            # Convert amount to grams and calculate nutrition
            nutrition = nutrition_data[ingredient]
            total_carbs += (nutrition["carbs"] / 100) * amount
            total_protein += (nutrition["protein"] / 100) * amount
    
    return total_carbs, total_protein

# Breakfast: 西红柿炒鸡蛋 (Tomato Scrambled Eggs)
# Standard portion: 1 tomato (180g), 1.5 eggs (75g), 6ml oil (5.5g), 2g salt, 1g sugar, 5g scallions
tomato_eggs_ingredients = {
    "西红柿": 180,
    "鸡蛋": 75,
    "食用油": 5.5,
    "盐": 2,
    "糖": 1,
    "葱花": 5
}

# Lunch: 荔枝肉 (Litchi Pork)
# Standard portion: 150g pork, 100g pineapple, 1 egg (50g), 500ml oil (460g), 5g sugar, 100g starch, 5ml soy sauce, 5g chicken essence, 5g ginger, 2g sesame, 20g tomato sauce, 2ml vinegar, 2 shiitake (30g), 30g crab mushroom
litchi_pork_ingredients = {
    "瘦肉": 150,
    "凤梨": 100,
    "鸡蛋": 50,
    "食用油": 460,
    "糖": 5,
    "淀粉": 100,
    "生抽": 5,
    "鸡精": 5,
    "姜": 5,
    "芝麻": 2,
    "番茄酱": 20,
    "香醋": 2,
    "鲜香菇": 30,
    "蟹味菇": 30
}

# Dinner: 葱油桂鱼 (Scallion Oil Mandarin Fish)
# Standard portion: 500g fish, 30g scallion, 2 peppers (20g), 50g ginger, 25g cooking wine, 15g oil, 8g salt, 10g soy sauce
scallion_fish_ingredients = {
    "桂鱼": 500,
    "小葱": 30,
    "小米辣": 20,
    "姜": 50,
    "料酒": 25,
    "植物油": 15,
    "盐": 8,
    "蒸鱼豉油": 10
}

# Calculate nutrition for each dish
breakfast_carbs, breakfast_protein = calculate_dish_nutrition(tomato_eggs_ingredients)
lunch_carbs, lunch_protein = calculate_dish_nutrition(litchi_pork_ingredients)
dinner_carbs, dinner_protein = calculate_dish_nutrition(scallion_fish_ingredients)

# Total daily nutrition
total_carbs = breakfast_carbs + lunch_carbs + dinner_carbs
total_protein = breakfast_protein + lunch_protein + dinner_protein

print("Nutritional Analysis:")
print(f"Breakfast (西红柿炒鸡蛋): Carbs: {breakfast_carbs:.1f}g, Protein: {breakfast_protein:.1f}g")
print(f"Lunch (荔枝肉): Carbs: {lunch_carbs:.1f}g, Protein: {lunch_protein:.1f}g")
print(f"Dinner (葱油桂鱼): Carbs: {dinner_carbs:.1f}g, Protein: {dinner_protein:.1f}g")
print(f"\nTotal Daily Intake:")
print(f"Carbohydrates: {total_carbs:.1f}g")
print(f"Protein: {total_protein:.1f}g")

# Compare with targets
carbs_min = 130.0
carbs_max = 162.5
protein_target = 97.5

print(f"\nTargets:")
print(f"Carbohydrates: {carbs_min:.1f}g - {carbs_max:.1f}g")
print(f"Protein: {protein_target:.1f}g")

# Assessment calculations
carbs_lower_bound = carbs_min * 0.95
carbs_upper_bound = carbs_max * 1.05

print(f"\nAssessment Ranges:")
print(f"Carbs below expectations: < {carbs_lower_bound:.1f}g")
print(f"Carbs excessive intake: > {carbs_upper_bound:.1f}g")
print(f"Protein below expectations: < {protein_target * 0.95:.1f}g")
print(f"Protein excessive intake: > {protein_target * 1.05:.1f}g") code
```
